</TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL"><B>Re:&nbsp;&nbsp;Supplemental Information Related to</B> <B><I>Item 3 &#150; Advisory Vote to Approve Executive Compensation </I></B>
</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">Dear Investor, </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">In the 2017 filing of Exxon Mobil Corporation&#146;s proxy, we
included an <I>Executive Compensation Overview</I> (<I>Overview</I>) as additional proxy material to summarize the key design features of our compensation program and demonstrate a strong linkage between ExxonMobil&#146;s compensation program and
business results. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">Charts 13 and 14 on page 7 of the <I>Overview</I> compare ExxonMobil CEO&#146;s compensation versus our compensation benchmark companies over a
10 year period from 2006 through 2015.</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">The 2016 data for our compensation benchmark companies have recently become available as they have filed their 2017 proxies.
Therefore we have updated both charts as shown below. This also updates all other references to these data in the <I>Overview</I>. </P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt" ALIGN="center">


<IMG SRC="g383474g60r21.jpg" ALT="LOGO">
 </P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:8pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">(1)</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">Realized Pay is compensation actually received by the CEO during the year, excluding any retirement distributions. Unrealized Pay represents the current value &#150; not the grant date value used for reporting in the
Summary Compensation Table&nbsp;&#150; of outstanding unvested cash and stock-based incentive awards as well as the current market value of unexercised &#147;in the money&#148; stock options granted during the years 2006 through 2016. Award values
are based on target levels of formula-based awards and fiscal <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-end</FONT> 2016 stock prices. Values for Caterpillar include estimates for fiscal <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-end</FONT> 2016 as the 2017
proxy had not been filed as of April&nbsp;19, 2017. See the back page of the <I>Executive Compensation Overview</I> for more detailed definitions of realized and unrealized pay. </TD></TR></TABLE>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:8pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">(2)</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">ExxonMobil CEO exercised last stock options granted in 2001 that would have expired in 2011. No stock options granted since 2001. </TD></TR></TABLE>
</DIV>


<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">


<DIV STYLE="width:7.25in" align="left">

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">Page 2 </P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<P STYLE="font-size:1pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">Pension and nonqualified deferred compensation data are excluded from the data included in both charts. However,
depending on how these values for the 2006 to 2016 period are determined, including pension value and nonqualified deferred compensation together with the realized pay and unrealized award values shown above would place the ExxonMobil CEO between
the 36th and the 67th percentiles among the compensation benchmark companies. Specifically: </P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman">&#9679;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">ExxonMobil CEO would rank at the 36th percentile if pension and nonqualified deferred compensation values are based on 11 years of average value per year of pension service (11 years represents the period from 2006
through 2016). </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:3%; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">For companies who have had more than one CEO during this period, the pension and nonqualified deferred compensation
values for both paid and accumulated amounts were averaged for this purpose, weighted by the tenure of the respective individual in the CEO position. Pension values are as reported in the Pension Benefits table. Nonqualified deferred compensation
values are as reported in the requisite table and may include executive contributions as well as company contributions and interest earned. </P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman">&#9679;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">ExxonMobil CEO would rank at the 67th percentile if pension value is simply calculated by aggregating the positive amounts shown in the annual &#147;Change in Pension Value and Nonqualified Deferred Compensation
Earnings&#148; column of the Summary Compensation Table for the covered period. </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL">We look forward to discussing this information with our shareholders
over the next several weeks and during the webinar on executive compensation and shareholder proposals on May&nbsp;11, 2017. </P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P><DIV ALIGN="right">
<TABLE CELLSPACING="0" CELLPADDING="0" WIDTH="40%" BORDER="0" STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:11pt">
